    if "(CLEntry.block_state (devcache1 T) = Modified ⟶ CLEntry.block_state (devcache2 T) ≠ Shared) ∧ (CLEntry.block_state (devcache2 T) = Modified ⟶ CLEntry.block_state (devcache1 T) ≠ Shared) ∧ (CLEntry.block_state (devcache1 T) = ISD ∧ htddatas1 T ≠ [] ⟶ CLEntry.block_state (devcache2 T) ≠ Modified) ∧ (CLEntry.block_state (devcache2 T) = ISD ∧ htddatas2 T ≠ [] ⟶ CLEntry.block_state (devcache1 T) ≠ Modified) ∧ (HostEntry.block_state (hostcache T) = SD ∧ dthdatas1 T ≠ [] ⟶ CLEntry.block_state (devcache1 T) ≠ Modified) ∧ (HostEntry.block_state (hostcache T) = SD ∧ dthdatas2 T ≠ [] ⟶ CLEntry.block_state (devcache2 T) ≠ Modified) ∧ (HostEntry.block_state (hostcache T) = SAD ∧ dthdatas1 T ≠ [] ⟶ CLEntry.block_state (devcache1 T) ≠ Modified) ∧ (HostEntry.block_state (hostcache T) = SAD ∧ dthdatas2 T ≠ [] ⟶ CLEntry.block_state (devcache2 T) ≠ Modified)"
